Ministry of Finance

Crack Down on Speculation in Margin Trading and Foreign Exchange

Exchanges Must Use Cash for Settlement

Order the Shanghai Exchange Supervisor to Comply

According to the Central News Agency, the Ministry of Finance issued instructions to the Shanghai Banking Association and the Exchange Supervisor yesterday to crack down on speculation in margin trading and foreign exchange, and sent a letter to the Central Bank to comply. The original text is recorded below: (A) Instruction: For compliance matters, it is found that foreign exchange trading, except for the following three items: (1) those necessary for legal and normal business; (2) those with contracts signed before September 8 of this year; (3) travel expenses or other private needs, all transactions shall be temporarily suspended from the date of this order. The Association should immediately inform the industry to comply accordingly. This order. (B) Official letter: Dear Sirs, it is found that foreign exchange trading, except for the following three items: (1) those necessary for legal and normal business; (2) those with contracts signed before September 8 of this year; (3) travel expenses or other private needs, all transactions shall be temporarily suspended from today. In addition to ordering the Shanghai Banking Association to comply, this letter is specially sent to your bank to quickly inform Chinese and foreign merchants and organizations to comply accordingly. To the Central Bank. In addition, an order was issued to the Shanghai Exchange Supervisor stating that the establishment of the exchange was originally to facilitate the trading of goods, but the Shanghai Gold Exchange has recently rarely settled in cash and mostly uses foreign exchange to settle prices, which not only violates the principle of gold trading but is also a place for speculators to create rumors and manipulate. In order to stabilize the market, this department urgently orders the supervisor to immediately order the exchange to use cash for all new transactions from the date of this order and not to use foreign exchange to settle prices, so as to match the name with the reality. The transactions made before may still be handled according to the original contract. The cash settlement shall also be supervised by the supervisor to organize a fineness appraisal committee to handle. In addition to informing the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, this order.

Eurasia's Large Aircraft

Hosted Various Circles for Day and Night Flights Yesterday

Flying Around the City, Wusong, Zhenru, and Fanwangdu

Mayor Wu and Zhu Jiaju were All on Space Night Flights

A New Record for Aviation in Shanghai Night Flight

Eurasia Aviation Corporation's newly arrived large aircraft, after arriving in Shanghai on the 6th, was well received by all circles in this city. The company's general manager, Mr. Li Jingzong, specially invited Mayor Wu Techeng, Minister of Communications Zhu Jiaju, German Minister Taodeman, and important figures from Chinese and foreign circles to test ride the day and night flights yesterday. A total of seven flights were flown starting at 3 p.m., each flight scheduled for a half-hour tour. Each flight was divided into 16 passengers, taking off from Hongqiao, along the Huangpu River, first to Wusong, and then circling the city, flying to Zhenru, Fanwangdu, and returning to the original place. It was a daytime flight to tour the entire Shanghai. Passengers included Wen Hongen, Director of the Municipal Public Safety Bureau, Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Works Bureau, Guo Shen, Secretary of the Municipal Government, Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Dr. Taodeman, the German Minister, totaling more than 120 people. In the evening, from 7 p.m. to 8:10 p.m., Mayor Wu Techeng of Shanghai, Minister of Communications Zhu Jiaju, and Li Jingzong himself, etc., took a night flight. When the plane took off, there was a red light on the nose and tail of the plane, and the electric lights inside the plane were also lit. When landing, because the Hongqiao Airport had no night flight landing light equipment, firewood and wood were burned around the airport as a marker. At the same time, the plane also opened the landing lights to illuminate the route. It was truly a new record for aviation in Shanghai night flight. All passengers praised it endlessly.

China Aviation Corporation Ordered from the United States

Dolphin Aircraft Shipped to Shanghai

Shanghai-Guangdong Line Scheduled to Resume Next Month

According to Shishi News Agency, China Aviation Corporation ordered two large Dolphin aircraft from the American Aviation Corporation, which have been shipped from the United States and are expected to arrive at the end of this month. The Shanghai-Guangdong Line has decided to resume operation starting next month. A reporter from Shishi News Agency specially explored and recorded the details as follows:

Dolphin Aircraft Shipped to Shanghai

In order to restore the Shanghai-Guangdong air route, China Aviation Corporation specially entrusted the American United Company to order two large Dolphin aircraft from the United States for application. According to a telegram received by China Aviation Corporation from the United States, the two aircraft have been manufactured by the United States and have been shipped to Shanghai, scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at the end of this month. The aircraft has a large fuselage and two motors, and can carry pilots and 10 passengers each time. The speed per hour is 150 kilometers. The aircraft is the latest product of the United States. The private aircraft used by the US President Roosevelt is also of this type. In order to maintain the safety of future flights, China Aviation Corporation has attached other safety equipment, which can also be used for blind flying at night to ensure safety. The pilots sent by the company to the United States to practice blind flying will also return home with the aircraft.

Shanghai-Guangdong Line Approved to Resume Next Month

China Aviation Corporation has been ordered by the Ministry of Communications to resume operation as soon as possible since the Shanghai-Guangdong line has been suspended for six months. Now that preparations have been completed, and after the new aircraft is shipped to Shanghai at the end of this month, the Shanghai-Guangdong line can be officially resumed next month. After the resumption of operation, the number of flights will be three times a week. The prices set are not much different from those previously set. At the same time, the establishment of meteorological stations and radio stations in the Hangzhou Bay area can also be completed in the shortest possible time.

Hubei Native Association

Called a Water and Drought Disaster Relief Meeting Yesterday

Elected Wu Xingya as Chairman of the Committee

And Passed Various Important Proposals

Chairman was Han Juemin, and the recorder was Zhao Puchu. The items discussed were as follows:

Passed Proposals

(1) All committee members passed ten articles of the detailed rules for the operation of the committee; (2) The two committee members Guan Jiongzhi and Yin Guanzhi proposed that the executive committee should mutually elect one chairman and two vice-chairmen. The proposal was passed; (3) Committee member Guan Jiongzhi proposed that each group should have several members in addition to the director, and the executive committee members should also serve as group members. The proposal was passed; (4) Committee member Yin Guanzhi proposed that the association should hold a meeting to welcome Minister Liu Wenzhou when he passes through Shanghai. The proposal was passed; (5) It was decided that the expenses of the association should be temporarily covered by the association.

Work Assignment

(1) Wu Xingya was elected as chairman, Guan Jiongzhi and Wang Shaoji were elected as vice-chairmen; (2) The following directors and vice-directors of each group were elected: (A) Director of the General Affairs Group: Han Juemin, Vice-Directors: Peng Yuncen, Hong Shiwei; (B) Director of the Fundraising Group: Wu Xingya, Vice-Directors: Jiong Guan, Yin Guanzhi; (C) Director of the Finance Group: Du Xiangqing, Vice-Directors: Mei Huanhou, Lu Xingjie; (D) Director of the Investigation Group: Yuan Xiaolan, Vice-Directors: Wang Shutang, Zhang Chuqiang. Sichuan Native Association

Telegraphed to Request Ways to Suppress the Exchange Rate

The Sichuan Native Association in Shanghai, due to the high exchange rate in Sichuan, has a great impact on the future of Sichuan merchants and students. They specially telegraphed Liu Xiang, the Sichuan authorities, to request that the exchange rate be maintained. The telegram said, urgent Chongqing Director Liu Pucheng Xunjian, members of our association in the business and academic circles have repeatedly stated that due to someone manipulating the exchange rate, the exchange rate from Chongqing to Shanghai has soared to 300 yuan per thousand yuan. Recently, there has been an upward trend. It is found that there are more outflows than inflows in Sichuan, and the export of cash is prohibited. The rise and fall of the exchange rate are normal, but if there is no manpower to manipulate it, it should not soar so much. Our association believes that this phenomenon is very harmful to Sichuan merchants and students outside the province. We specially telegraphed you, please use the consistent principle of Anchuan and benefiting the people, and the responsibility of leading the group, to take effective measures to stop the manipulation and suppress the exchange rate, so that merchants do not suspend business, and students do not stop chanting, then the hometown will be fortunate. Sichuan Native Association in Shanghai, Jia Yin.

Going to Rural Areas in the Country for Exhibition

County Agricultural Education Center

Please County Government to Prohibit Slaughtering of Plough Cattle

The Zhuangqiao Farmer Education Center in Shanghai County has paid much attention to the care of plough cattle in recent years. This year, the weather has been extremely arid and the plough cattle are extremely tired. The time has come to the White Dew Festival, and there is a custom among the people to slaughter cattle for food, which is not in line with human feelings and legal principles. The center held its 17th rural improvement meeting yesterday and discussed it. It was unanimously advocated that a petition be submitted to the county government to strictly prohibit it. The center has already prepared a document to petition County Magistrate Pan to issue a prohibition. The document says that there is a custom among the people to slaughter plough cattle for food after the White Dew Festival every year. It is believed that plough cattle are important livestock for farmers. They help with plowing in spring and summer and endure all kinds of hardships. When the agricultural gap arrives, they should be properly cared for to reward their previous labor and restore the health of the cattle. Even if funds are needed, they can be borrowed for application. It is inhumane to kill them suddenly, and the slaughter of plough cattle is prohibited by law. The central, provincial and county governments have repeatedly ordered and emphasized it, but ignorant people still cannot avoid disobeying the law. The center held its 17th rural improvement meeting on the 5th of this month, and unanimously advocated that a petition be submitted to the county government to issue a strict prohibition. For this reason, a document is prepared and submitted to you for your review and approval, and a strict prohibition is issued to rectify the people's hearts and maintain agricultural administration. Both public and private interests will be benefited.

Franco-Italian Accord

British Public Opinion Mixed

(London) Recently, newspapers have been widely reporting that an agreement will be established between France and Italy, causing public opinion to be unusually excited. Although the rumor that France and Italy have established an anti-German military agreement was denied by official circles in Paris, claiming that Franco-Italian negotiations have not yet produced concrete results, this is difficult to believe here. For example, The Times claimed that France and Italy had long been alarmed by Germany's rearmament and were considering ways to defend themselves. The newspaper also criticized Germany's abandonment of the League of Nations policy, but stated that the establishment of an understanding between France and Italy is also quite difficult, the biggest obstacle being the friendship between France and Yugoslavia. As for the Franco-Italian naval agreement, the newspaper felt even more doubtful. The Daily Telegraph's political correspondent, however, stated that an understanding had been reached between France and Italy regarding the naval presence of both countries off the coast of Libya and the colonization of Tunisians in Italy, which was welcome news in London. However, regarding the so-called military agreement, it was said that it should not be fully believed yet. The Rome correspondent for the Morning Post stated that the negotiations between France and Italy do not aim to encircle Germany and establish a military agreement. The newspaper expressed great welcome to the solid friendship between France and Italy. (National Telegram, 8th)

False Alarm in Vienna

Inattentive National Guard Accidentally Fires Rifle

People Suspect Assassination Attempt on Austrian Deputy Chancellor

Vienna Today, the people here are quite anxious, as an event occurred that was initially thought to be an assassination attempt on Deputy Chancellor Prince Starhemberg. This afternoon, from the house opposite Starhemberg's residence, someone suddenly fired a gun at it, and the bullet hit the wall of a room downstairs. Police and National Guardsmen immediately rushed to the scene, surrounded the area where the gun was fired, and searched house to house, thinking it must be the work of the communists, as the communists have been unusually active recently. However, nothing was found. Finally, it was learned that the gun was accidentally fired by a member of the National Guard. It is said that he was inattentive and bumped his rifle against the wall of the room opposite Starhemberg's residence, causing it to go off. Fearing severe punishment at the time, he did not immediately admit it. The entire city has now returned to normal. (Reuters Dispatch, 8th)

Mussolini Again Advocates the Yellow Peril Theory

Saying That European Countries Must Unite

To jointly resist Japan's monopoly of the Far East

A special telegram from the Osaka Asahi Shimbun in Rome on the 3rd of this month reported that Prime Minister Mussolini recently issued the Japanese Yellow Peril theory, saying that although Italy's territorial interests in the Far East are relatively light, from an economic point of view, the current situation in the Far East cannot be ignored. The shipment of Japanese goods in the Eastern market is quite amazing, and Italy's artificial silk exports have been overwhelmed, because today Italy, in the world the position of the second country of artificial silk will be won by Japan, and even silk, cotton and other Japanese goods, also invaded the Italian market, etc. Originally, Mr. Mussolini, although politically advocated the integration of Eastern and Western cultures, he is quite vigilant against the real problems, because he fears that Japan will monopolize hegemony in the Far East and develop the power of Japanese imperialism, so he loudly calls for the promotion of the Yellow Peril theory to warn European countries, hoping to unite the common front to confront Japan, and said that European countries in the Far East must not turn against each other, so that Japan can take advantage of it and reap the benefits of the fisherman, and should inform Japan of the limits that should be observed, and if Japan does not agree, then unite the European countries to confront it.

Germany's New Economic Policy

Earnestly Implement Agricultural Policies to Save Unemployed People

Equal Emphasis on Local Economy and Outward Development of Commerce

And Advocates Moving Urban People to Rural Areas to Increase Production

National News Agency German Correspondent, since the German National Socialist Party took power, it has not only been able to reform the political state, but also the economic state, and has also been vigorously reformed. According to the facts, the implementation of the reform of economic policies has been quite effective, so Germany's economic policy has a great relationship with the world, and the National Socialist Party is doing its best to study the methods of reform. If the economic position changes, Germany's international position will also be different, so it must be carefully considered. Today's unemployment problem, if all countries in the world can solve it, then the world's economic and political situation should gradually become prosperous, but it must be noted that the unemployment problem is caused by the current economic turnover and changes in economic organization. Since the war, whether in Germany or Britain, the export of its industrial products has not been able to restore the state before the war, and the export amount of industrial products before the war has often increased, but now it has not been increased in fact, so the unemployment problem has gradually expanded, so that when the economy directly changes during and after the war, each consumer country also sets up factories and starts manufacturing, so that the export products are not as good as before, the sales are decreasing, and the income is sharply reduced.

Because of these undisguisable facts, the National Socialist Party used it as a warning for economic planning. Now, the National Socialist Party is devoting itself to foreign trade and proceeding step by step to enrich the domestic economy in order to achieve its goals in the shortest possible time, so that the national economy will not be chaotic, and the Germans must be under the pressure of this helpless fact, to relieve the internal and external economic difficulties. In this way, the Germans cannot break away from the world economy, and it must be known that solving the domestic economic problems cannot be without any contact with the world, but must focus on the domestic economy. However, foreign trade should never be neglected. As for the trade relations with a certain country, it should be more or less, depending on the trade situation of each country.

The problem discussed here is how to solve Germany's internal economic problems, and its focus is on earnestly implementing the agricultural policy plan. The Germans now need to reorganize the local economy, and the outward-looking commercial policy should be earnestly implemented, so that they can obtain a large amount of benefits, so as to reduce the number of unemployed people, and in the future, wages will not be reduced, and the consolidation of wages will not be shaken. If this goal is to be achieved, everyone must have the idea of outward development, so that the unemployed can be re-employed, and they can work hard, and there are jobs everywhere. In this plan, we can enable a large number of unemployed people to be re-employed, so the purchasing power of the people can be improved.

Now, the Germans must first understand that this is not to reorganize the local economy, but to build big cities with one heart, but to go from big cities to small cities, in other words, to consolidate the importance of the economy according to the needs of the local area, but whether this can succeed can only be known afterwards. The National Socialist Party's economic plan varies from time to time and place to place, and it is actively responsible for implementing it. If this kind of plan can be realized, the world economy will inevitably be affected. The National Socialist Party always remembers and never forgets that it wants to reduce 150,000 unemployed people in the shortest possible time, which is the biggest undertaking, and by this, the purchasing power can be improved, so that Germany's internal economy will be prosperous day by day, and develop to infinity. But in this, there must be an overall comprehensive idea, and the National Socialist Party's plan also extends to other matters, that is, the reorganization of the economy is not purely within the scope of the economy, and in addition, attention is paid to political and cultural undertakings, so the National Socialist Party has not neglected economic and cultural undertakings. As for the eastern part of Germany, because the population is sparse, so that it has not been operated for a long time, there is a great danger in politics, so immigration should also be implemented. The more people from the cities move into the rural areas, the more natural products will be produced. This kind of undertaking is very big, and the national livelihood problem is even more important. The National Socialist Party's economic plan is to strive for step-by-step rationality and to be suitable for the principles of implementation, and it has unprecedented ability.

Collapse of the Yellow River Beach

Top Impact of Mud in Zhongmu, Henan Collapses by More Than Five Zhang

Yellow River Commission Asks for Immediate Allocation of 30,000 Yuan for Emergency Relief

Kaifeng Correspondence, at this time last year, the Yellow River water situation was already stable, but this year's situation is different. Today's comprehensive report from various hydrological stations, Tongguan at 1:00 p.m., water level 321.84 meters, flow rate 2800 cubic meters per second, Shanzhou at noon, water level 292.58 meters, flow rate 2850 cubic meters per second, Zhengzhou Qin Factory at noon, water level 945.66 meters, flow rate 7500 cubic meters per second, an increase of 2 centimeters from the 5th, Heigangkou increased by 1.4 centimeters, Liuyuankou increased by 1.6 centimeters, the engineer of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission stationed in the Hebei River Affairs Bureau for coordination and defense, He Youliang branch (4th) telegrammed that in the Fenglou Village area, the main current moved north, starting from 60 meters east of Yanggeng Temple, collapsing. In the past two days, the beach dam has been scoured, about 50 meters wide and 2 kilometers long, and it is still collapsing. The situation is urgent and dangerous. It is planned to selectively grab Liujuan to defend it. Yanggeng Dam has not yet leaned on the current, and it is feared that the current will rise to the embankment. It is estimated that raising the top of the dam and disaster relief requires 30,000 yuan. The Hebei Provincial Treasury is empty, and I beg you to forward it to the Executive Yuan to find a way to provide assistance, etc. After Li Yizhi received the telegram, he has forwarded it to the Executive Yuan today to allocate funds for emergency relief. The top impact of the eight forts and six dams in Shangfan, Zhongmu, collapsed by 5.5 zhang long and 7 chi wide on the 5th. The Shangnan Branch rushed to hang willows and parse them at the head of the dam, and moved dozens of square meters of nearby stored stones to protect them, but they have not yet come out of the water. Chen Ruzhen, accompanied by Tan Zheng, Mu Lingyuan, etc., went to supervise the filling and plugging today. Although the protection was thrown day and night, the situation has not improved (6th).

Reading News

Issue 26 Compiled by the Shenbao Circulation Library Reading Guidance Department

Table of Contents... My Reading Experience - Gao Er Reading Q&A Voting Results Public Mailbox

My Reading Experience

I am a child from a poor family, so naturally I could not enter any new schools. From a young age in my hometown, I managed to study for nine years, reciting the Three Character Classic and the Hundred Family Surnames, and recognizing a few characters. When I was sixteen, because my family was poor, I left my parents and came to Shanghai to work as an apprentice. During the three-year apprenticeship, I often had the opportunity to read newspapers and the popular romance novels of the Mandarin Ducks and Butterflies School at that time. However, these books and newspapers were not of much benefit to me, because they were all about the love lives of young masters, or things like dark secrets. In addition, the words and allusions used in those books made me feel confused when I read them. Because I didn't have that kind of life, I couldn't understand the original meaning of the books and couldn't arouse my interest. Later, I felt that these books were not for apprentices like us, so I stopped reading them. Later, I started reading books on chemistry, physics, and other subjects related to my work. Although I didn't understand many terms, because these books were in line with the needs of my daily work, I felt a little interested and gained some benefit. The three years of apprenticeship quickly passed, and then I felt the problems of life and the problems of humanity. Under this mood, I began to read social science books. Unfortunately, there were not many social science books at that time, and even if there were, they were written in classical Chinese. Although I read them, I didn't feel interested or gain any benefit. This was naturally because I didn't understand classical Chinese. Later, I stopped reading books, but although I stopped on the surface, I was still passionately pursuing knowledge in my heart. Under this circumstance, after finishing work every day, when I went to sleep, I always thought slowly about the things I encountered and saw during the day, and I wanted to figure out a reason for them, otherwise I couldn't sleep. Sometimes I couldn't solve it myself, so I asked others and discussed it with them. In this way, I gradually felt interested, which was more practical than reading a book. For example, when I thought of the boss's abuse of apprentices, I always resented them for being inhuman in the past. Later, I saw in a deeper level that this was not a phenomenon in our store alone. It turned out that society was a part of people abusing another part of people. The boss was not humane or inhumane. All the crows in the world are equally black: if I were the boss, I would do the same. So I thought that this was not a problem of one person. However, the understanding at that time was more superficial than what I am saying now. Naturally, I still felt insufficient. I still wanted to find books to read when I had time. However, at this time, I already knew that reading books should be in line with our actual life and not waste time. So before I read books, I thought of the following questions: 1. What books should we read? 2. What books are in line with our actual life? 3. What books can help us live? The above three questions are my reading experience. I often ask myself these questions. In this way, I gradually understood that reading dead books is useless. Knowledge must be sought in actual life. The things that exist in society are all materials for our research. Books are just reference books for our research of these materials. Everything in the world has its reasons and conditions for existence. As long as we study it calmly, we can always find its cause and effect relationship. (Manuscript from Gao Er)

Public Mailbox

(1) Recently, the replies from this department have often been delayed for up to a month, which has caused many readers to express well-intentioned reproaches. This makes us feel very sorry! The replies from this department, except for those that are prepared to be published in the "Reading Q&A," have always been for ordinary questions. Replies can be sent within a week. Requests for application forms, etc., can be sent within three days. More specialized questions that require consulting many books must also be answered within two weeks at the latest. However, for those questions that the colleagues in this department cannot answer, this department will send them to specially contracted experts, or temporarily find others to answer them. The time will inevitably be extended. This time, two letters were delayed for up to forty days because they were sent to a certain gentleman for an answer last month. The gentleman left Shanghai due to an event, and repeatedly entrusted others to forward them. In the end, the original letters were returned. This department found someone else to answer them, setting an unprecedented precedent. In the future, we will firmly adhere to our previous decision. The general principle for replying to letters is one week. For those that cannot be answered within one week, we will send a separate card to inform the reader, so as to avoid the reader's anxious anticipation. (2) If readers raise more than one question, they must also consider the nature of the questions, based on the principle of similarity. If you casually ask about everything from heaven to earth, it is difficult for us to answer. It would be convenient for everyone if you divide the miscellaneous questions into several times to ask. (3) All the procedures for participating in this department are detailed in the library catalog compilation of this library. Each catalog sells for seven cents in foreign currency. It is sold at the fee collection office of this library. For out-of-town inquiries, please attach seven cents in postage stamps to be mailed. (4) The publication date of Reading News has been changed. This column, Reading News, was originally published every Tuesday. Starting this week, it will be published every Monday. We hope readers will pay attention! The manuscript "Explaining Contradictions" has not yet been fully published. It will continue to be published on Tuesday.

Special Article

Reducing Railway Freight Rates and Developing the Rural Economy (6) Wu Shaozeng 8

During last year's harvest season, the total amount of rice transported upstream on the entire Beijing-Shanghai line was only over 6,000 metric tons, accounting for a very small percentage of the total output. Moreover, most of these 6,000 metric tons were transported only within the scope of this railway. Only over 1,660 metric tons were transported to the north of the Yangtze River, which is less than 28% of the total. This is also sufficient to prove that long-distance transportation is not thriving.

(3) On the consumption side, a balance between supply and demand is a good sign for everything, especially for agricultural products that are related to people's livelihood. If the supply exceeds the demand at the consumption site of agricultural products, then the price will fall, which will make the farmers' hard work unrewarding. Conversely, if the demand exceeds the supply, then the price will be high. Farmers may profit from it, but other sectors will have a feeling of difficult life, which is not appropriate. However, China has long become the end of the world, and the self-sufficiency of various places in the country is insufficient, creating opportunities for foreign goods. Therefore, agricultural countries have the strange phenomenon of relying on foreign countries for agricultural products. According to the import statistics of rice, flour, and cotton in 1920, they are as follows:

Rice 19,921,1918 (shi) 121,244,766 (customs taels)

Flour 5,150,307 (dan) 31,556,388 (customs taels)

Cotton 3,474,889 (dan) 133,135,567 (customs taels)

The total import value of the three items is slightly less than 286 million customs taels. In addition, the value of imported foreign dried fruits, according to the statistics for December 1922, reached 330,000 gold yuan, which is more than 4 million gold yuan annually, which is more than 12 million national currency. What is its impact on our rural economy? Tracing the reason, it is nothing more than the excess supply in the main production areas and the excess demand in the main consumption areas. The reason for this imbalance between supply and demand is that traffic is blocked and freight is high. Otherwise, even if we sometimes rely on foreign countries, the quantity will definitely not be so huge. This can be asserted.

To sum up, for the sake of helping to develop the rural economy, the railway has a real need to thoroughly revise the freight rates for most agricultural products. It seems that the Ministry of Railways may as well designate several kinds of domestic agricultural products that are important to people's livelihood, economy, or national defense, and set a uniform and low freight rate that is beyond everything, leaving the transportation cost aside. That is,

According to the grades, respectively stipulate the freight rate per 100 kilometers per metric ton (whole vehicle) or per 50 kilograms (less than a whole vehicle), how much per 200 kilometers, how much per 300 kilometers, how much per 400 kilometers, how much per 500 kilometers, (less than 100 kilometers are all calculated according to 100 kilometers) (500 kilometers or more, regardless of distance, all are calculated according to 500 kilometers. Whether it is transportation on this railway or joint transportation on various railways, all are handled in accordance with this. As for the formulation of freight rates, the following steps can be taken:

(1) Investigate the inherent cost of each type of agricultural product, (2) Investigate the ordinary market price of each type of domestic agricultural product, (3) Investigate the selling price of imported foreign agricultural products of the same value, (4) Appropriately determine the minimum freight rate for each type of agricultural product per metric ton (whole vehicle) or per 50 kilograms (less than a whole vehicle) for transporting 100 kilometers, 200 kilometers, 300 kilometers, 400 kilometers, and 500 kilometers, so that the sum of the production cost and freight of each type of agricultural product does not exceed the ordinary market price of each city and can compete with imported foreign agricultural products of the same value. (5) Appropriately determine the percentage that should be increased for every 100 kilometers added between 100 kilometers and 500 kilometers (be sure to take a percentage that is easy to calculate). (To be continued)

Slaughter Tax and Brokerage Tax Collection and Transfer in Shanghai and Nanjing

The Special Education Fund Case in Jiangsu Province is Fully Resolved

The slaughter tax and brokerage tax in Jiangsu Province's education funding, amounting to approximately 1.3 million yuan annually, account for slightly less than one-third of the province's education funding. Since the establishment of the special municipalities of Shanghai and Nanjing, the slaughter tax and brokerage tax collected in the municipal areas have been designated by the Jiangsu education sector as a special education fund and cannot be transferred, affecting the inherent education cause of the entire Jiangsu Province. The Ministry of Education has convened meetings of responsible representatives from the province and municipalities for discussions, and the Executive Yuan has decided that since the funds are designated for provincial education, these two types of tax revenue should still be managed by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office. Subsequently, the province and municipalities negotiated back and forth. Nanjing agreed that the municipal government would collect and transfer an annual slaughter tax of 30,000 yuan and a brokerage tax of 14,000 yuan, and the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office has already resolved to follow this. Shanghai has agreed that the municipal government will collect and transfer an annual slaughter tax of 70,000 yuan, and this has also been resolved. However, for the brokerage tax, the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office and the Shanghai Municipal Government recently agreed on a contract in late August that the Shanghai Municipal Government will collect an annual sum of 42,000 yuan and transfer it on a monthly basis. The municipal government and the management office will each stamp and hold a copy of the agreed-upon method to ensure credibility. The long-standing dispute between the two municipalities of Shanghai and Nanjing and the Jiangsu provincial education authorities over the slaughter tax and brokerage tax case has now been fully resolved. The agreed-upon method between the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office is excerpted below: (1) The Shanghai Municipal Government will take over the collection and transfer of brokerage tax from Shanghai and Baoshan, which are incorporated into the municipal area, starting from July 1, 1934. (2) After the municipal government takes over this brokerage tax, it will allocate a regular tax amount of 42,000 yuan annually to the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office to maintain the special education fund. (3) This brokerage tax will be collected and transferred monthly by the municipal government according to the fixed amount, with 3,500 yuan allocated to the management office each month for receipt. (Several other articles, which ensure the method for this special education fund and the date of transfer of funds, are omitted.)

Addendum

It is found that the column for students from the previous joint entrance exam in the 22nd academic year who did not finish the senior high school graduation joint entrance exam but passed all three subjects after the make-up exam and should be allowed to graduate was missing the name of Yin Mei-gu from McTyeire School, which should be added. Also, in the column for senior high school joint entrance exam students who failed three or more subjects, Shi Xue-wu from the Hujiang University Affiliated Middle School and Chen Jing-chao from the Qiaoguang Middle School were mistakenly reported by their schools to have missed their Biology and Mathematics grades, respectively. After the original schools submitted supplementary reports, they were approved for review and passed. The students should be listed in the column for students who failed one subject and should be corrected accordingly.

Jiangsu Provincial Elementary School Association

Experimental Research Committee Held a Meeting Yesterday

Representatives from Various Schools Attended, Totaling More Than [Unclear]

Discussing the Unified Control of Experimental Research Work

The Experimental Research Committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Elementary School Association held a meeting starting at 9:00 AM yesterday at the Provincial Shanghai Experimental Elementary School. Details are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives

Principal Shen Shan-zhi of Zhenjiang Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, Principal Pan Yi-shan of Wuxi Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, Principal Wu Zeng-jie of Suzhou Women's Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, Principal Chen Zhen-e of Rugao Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, Principal Sheng Lang-xi of Shanghai Experimental Elementary School, and experimental research directors from each school, including Jin Run-qing, Xu Jie-ping, Jiang Bing-long, Jiang Pin-zhen, Xu Chang-lin, Zhu Jing-xing, Shi Zhi-qing, Zhu Wei-zhang, and more than twenty others, attended.

Reports from Each School

Representatives from each school registered one after another at 9:00 AM. The meeting officially commenced at [Unclear] o'clock, chaired by Standing Committee Member Sheng Lang-xi, with Shi Zhi-qing and Zhu Wei-zhang recording. The chairman first reported the purpose of the meeting and then passed the organizational regulations. Representatives from each school then reported on the main points of their respective experimental research programs for the year 1934 as follows: (1) Suzhou Women's Normal School Affiliated Elementary School is piloting design teaching methods in lower grades, complex group divisions in middle grades, and self-study guidance in higher grades. (2) Wuxi Normal School Affiliated Elementary School is piloting design teaching methods in lower grades, a curriculum starting from rural areas in middle grades, and scout-centered education in higher grades. (3) Suzhou Women's Normal School is implementing individual learning, experimenting with local education, compiling lower-grade activity-centered curricula, implementing scientific training, and implementing production training. (4) Songjiang Elementary School continues to implement national defense education teaching. (5) Suzhou Experimental Elementary School is piloting design teaching methods in lower grades and voluntary learning in middle and upper grades. (6) Yangzhou Experimental Elementary School is piloting activity-centered teaching methods in lower grades and group self-study methods in middle and upper grades. (7) Zhenjiang Normal School Affiliated Elementary School is researching the minimum teaching standards for each subject in local elementary schools, reviewing the Chinese language curriculum, and conducting a general survey of elementary schools in each county. (8) Rugao Normal School Affiliated Elementary School is piloting extracurricular reading and focusing on individual guidance research. (9) Shanghai Experimental Elementary School is experimenting with methods of national salvation education, repeatedly implementing strict training, group training, and production training. In terms of teaching methods, it is piloting continuous whole-class teaching in lower grades, continuous problem-based teaching in middle grades, and continuous individual teaching in upper grades.

Continued Discussion of Proposals

Continued discussion of the tasks assigned by the General Assembly: (1) Regarding the proposal on how to unify and control the experimental research work of each committee of this association, it was resolved that: A. Summaries of the experimental research work reported by representatives of each school should be collected and submitted to the standing committee for consolidation. B. Each school should be required to submit an outline of the experimental research plan within one month, which will be compiled and distributed by the standing committee to each school. The results of the experimental research should also be collected on schedule and submitted to the standing committee for consolidation and publication. (2) Regarding the proposal to assign responsibility for creating or reforming standard tests and scales, it was resolved that: 1. Nanjing Experimental Elementary School, Zhenjiang Experimental Elementary School, and Zhenjiang Normal School Affiliated Elementary School should be invited to take charge of drafting preliminary implementation methods. 2. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education should be requested to provide guidance, and academic groups such as the Chinese Education Society, the Chinese Testing Society, the China Children's Education Society, the Education College of Central University, the Education College of Daxia University, and the Jiangsu Provincial Education College should be invited to cooperate. (3) The proposal to establish minimum graduation standards for elementary schools was resolved to be carried out after the standard tests are compiled. (4) Regarding the proposal to stipulate the types and formats of children's notebooks for each subject, it was resolved to follow the "Workbook and Form Special Issue" in the Elementary School Teachers' Volume. (5) Regarding the proposal to request experts to provide guidance on all ongoing work, it was resolved to request Mr. Chen Shi-dong, Mr. Ai Xian-zhou, Mr. Luo Ting-guang, Mr. Liao Mao-ru, Mr. Chen Xuan-shan, Mr. Chen He-qin, Mr. Xiao Xiao-rong, Mr. [Unclear] Li-jiang, and other gentlemen to serve as instructors. (6) Regarding the proposal for each school to cooperate fully in research and statistical work, it was resolved that each school in this association has the obligation to provide materials and complete survey forms for each other. The meeting concluded at 3:00 PM, and in the evening, the editorial committee of the China Children's Education Society hosted a banquet at the Laixi Restaurant on Xiaoshadu Road in Jing'an Temple.

Groundbreaking Ceremony for Guangzhao Middle School's New Campus

The groundbreaking ceremony for Guangzhao Middle School's new campus was held yesterday morning at the new site on Shuiding Road. Mayor Wu, Wen Hong-en, Chen Bing-qian, Guo Le, Guo Shun, Li Da-chao, Lao Jing-xiu, Tang Bao-shu, Yang Run-zhi, Situ Shang-shen, and more than two thousand people attended.

Photo of Mayor Wu Performing the Groundbreaking Ceremony (Taken by Wang Kai) 10

People. The military band of the Public Security Bureau attended and played music, and the ceremony was conducted in accordance with etiquette. Chairman Chen Bing-qian reported on the preparations, construction, and land purchase process, as well as the current progress plan. Mayor Wu then performed the groundbreaking ceremony and delivered auspicious words. Mayor Wu stated that the school was the largest school established by Cantonese people in Shanghai and bore an extraordinarily important mission, which depended on the efforts and cooperation of all fellow villagers. Therefore, after delivering the auspicious words for the groundbreaking ceremony, he made an extremely sincere and concise speech, which deeply moved the listeners. Guo Shun then gave a speech, also earnestly encouraging everyone to complete the school's expansion plan. The school was approved by the Ministry of the Interior to requisition 100 mu of private land for use. The first phase should purchase 100 mu of land, and more than 90 mu have already been purchased. The first phase of construction is also expected to be completed by the end of September.

Broadcast Lecture by the Municipal Education Bureau

Commissioner Zhou Lectures on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's First Uprising

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education broadcast a lecture at the Zhongxi Pharmacy Radio Station at 4:30 PM the day before yesterday, in which Mr. Yuan Zeng-yu from the bureau spoke about the Eight-Nation Alliance and the signing of the Boxer Protocol. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the bureau continued to broadcast a lecture at the same radio station, in which Commissioner Zhou lectured on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's first uprising, giving a detailed account of the circumstances of Dr. Sun's uprising at the time, as well as the significance of today's commemoration.

Recent Situation of Shen Bao Evening School

Although the Shen Bao Evening School has only been in operation for a year and a half, due to the efforts of the staff and the low tuition fees, more than 1,500 people enrolled for the new semester this summer by the closing date of the 6th of this month. After the placement test, they were divided into 59 classes of German, Russian, Japanese, English, Bookkeeping, and Chinese, with both advanced and beginner levels. In addition to continuing to employ the original excellent teachers, the new teachers hired this summer are all highly specialized and experienced, and the students are benefiting greatly. It is also heard that there are still a few vacancies, and enrollment will continue from the 11th.

Sports News 11

Advanced Singles Quarterfinals

Qiu Feihai Wins Against Zheng Zhaojia After a Fierce Battle

A Five-Set Thriller Lasts Over Two Hours Before a Victor Emerges

Zheng Loses After Leading 5-1 in the Fifth Set

▲ China Loses to the United States in the Robber Cup Quarterfinals

Results of the advanced singles quarterfinals in lawn tennis: Karlson easily defeats Mada in straight sets; Qiu Feihai wins a five-set thriller against Zheng Zhaojia, lasting over two hours. Zheng had many opportunities to win but failed due to a lack of experience. Zheng led 5-1 in the first set but then lost six consecutive games, losing the set 5-7. In the fifth set, Zheng again led 5-1, and in the next game, with Qiu serving, Zheng was down 1-3 (15-40). Zheng only needed one more point to defeat Qiu Feihai. However, at this critical juncture, he failed to capitalize, losing point after point, and the score was tied 5-5. Qiu finally won the last set 9-7. In the Robber Cup China-U.S. match continuation, only five games were played, with the U.S. winning the fifth game 9-7. The U.S.-Portugal match was postponed due to darkness. The results of each group are as follows:

(Advanced Singles) Karlson (6-2, 6-0, 6-3) Mada

(Advanced Singles) Qiu Feihai (7-5, 6-4, 5-7, 3-6, 9-7) Zheng Zhaojia

(Robber Cup Match) Karlson, Squia (6-4, 9-7, 8-10, 2-6, 9-7) Lin Baohua, Qiu Feihai

Robber Cup China-U.S. Match Continuation

In the Robber Cup quarterfinals, China and the United States each won two sets yesterday. The fifth set was stopped due to darkness when the score was 5-5. The match continued yesterday at the French Chamber of Commerce. Both sides were cautious and did not dare to act rashly. Qiu Feihai won a game with his serve, and his opponent Squia also won with his serve. Lin Baohua won again with his serve, and Karlson tied the score again, making it 7-7. In the next game, with Qiu serving, he won the first three points but ultimately failed, and the U.S. took the lead 8-7. Squia's serve game relied on three successful net interceptions by Shi, and China lost 7-9.

Karlson Defeats Mada

In the advanced singles quarterfinals, the outcome of Karlson versus Mada was expected. Karlson easily won in straight sets, losing only five games. Mada, who qualified for the quarterfinals due to Lin Baohua's withdrawal, performed mediocrely and had nothing to offer.

Qiu Feihai Narrowly Wins Against Little Zheng

Qiu Feihai Escapes Death. Qiu Feihai versus Zheng Zhaojia was the third group to take the stage. The two players' skills were evenly matched, but Zheng lacked experience. He was either very good or very bad. His momentum was loose, his ball speed was slow, and his interest was very low. After the start, Zheng quickly took a 5-1 lead. Qiu followed closely, merely parrying without attacking, knowing Zheng's weaknesses and wanting to wait for him to self-destruct. Initially, Zheng was quite smooth, with very few self-destructions, so he was able to cruise along. However, later it was not like that. He repeatedly sent the ball into the net, allowing Qiu Feihai to win without effort, winning six consecutive games and reversing the lead to 7-5. In the second set, Qiu took a 3-1 lead, Zheng tied it at 3-3, 4-4, and finally Qiu still won 6-4.

Zheng Zhaojia Strives and Achieves. In the third set, Zheng performed the best, and Qiu also stepped up his game, making the situation tense. After 2-2, Zheng used a heavy serve, immediately followed by a net rush, winning four consecutive points and making Qiu helpless. Zheng also gained an advantage in Qiu's serve game with the above net rush, making it 4-2, and Zheng took the upper hand. Qiu also retaliated fiercely, no longer waiting for Zheng to self-destruct like before. Before long, Qiu reversed the score to 5-4. Zheng refused to be outdone and won three consecutive games, taking back a set 7-5. After a break, Zheng won easily 6-3 in one go, and Qiu Feihai's face showed fatigue.

Qiu Feihai Receives an Unexpected Harvest. The fifth set was a matter of life and death. Zheng won the first two games, and Qiu won back one game. In Zheng's serve game, one person had an extremely beautiful diagonal shot, earning a lot of applause, which was the most exciting part. Zheng's momentum was strong, and he won three more games, taking a distant lead of 5-1. Qiu Feihai's spirit was dim, and he was at a loss. Zheng's final victory seemed to be in his grasp, and in the next game, with Qiu serving, he was already down 1-3. Zheng only needed to win one more point to resolve the victory or defeat. It was thought that Qiu would admit defeat. Who knew that Zheng would self-destruct again and again, sending even the easiest balls into the net, while Qiu was as steady as usual. Although he could not use fierce shots, he could at least return the ball over the net. Zheng repeated the mistakes of the first set and was beaten by Qiu to 5-5. Qiu served, and Zheng won four straight, thinking that Zheng could still win. In this set, the next game was Zheng's serve, but who knew he would also lose his serve, making it 6-6. Qiu then gained the advantage with a serve game, reversing to 7-6. Although Zheng made it 7-7, he ultimately failed 7-9. Alas, the sky was getting dark, and the Anglo-Portuguese Robber Cup doubles could not be held and was postponed.

Spring and Autumn

Xiaoxitian 12

— Original by Princess Deling, Translated by Qin Shouou

Chapter 1: Ghosts Carry a Cartload of Guests from Guanzhong; A Family with Only Four Walls Crosses the River, Lamenting People from Qin

Secretary Chang said: "The common people can't find anything on the land. They can't just starve to death. Naturally, they have to exchange things for money to buy food. When it comes to exchanging for money, what else do the villagers have besides clothes and farm tools? City people don't want farm tools. The countryside can't grow land, and everyone is poor, so no one buys farm tools. As for clothes, people here can wear one piece of clothing for half a lifetime. Even if they sell them, there are no clothes to sell. So they only have two ways to exhaust their resources: one is to sell their livestock, and the other is to tear down windows, door panels, and roof beams, push them into the city in carts, and sell them. Tearing down roof beams to sell is the last resort for villagers. Once they sell them, they flee the famine. When one family leaves the village, another is torn down. Some people don't have time to tear them down and leave early. Later, some people will do it for them, so the village often becomes a strange phenomenon of only walls and no houses. Because of this, the people of Shaanxi have provided great proof of the ancient saying describing poor people as having nothing but the four walls of their homes. Truly, their homes only have four bare walls." Cheng Zhiqian said: "Is it really that bad? It's been six or seven years since the great drought of the eighteenth year. How hasn't it recovered yet?" Secretary Chang said: "How easy is it?" Saying that, he shook his head twice and said, "This can't be explained in a few words." Zhang Jiefu heard this and thought that it would be better to find a position in the provincial capital. The outer counties might be too difficult. Li Shilian also thought that the place was so poor that the common people definitely wouldn't eat meat, smoke, or drink wine casually. The slaughter tax and tobacco and alcohol tax probably wouldn't be very promising. When Cheng Zhiqian heard that the countryside was so poor, he paid extra attention to the situation along the way. Zhang and Li also had their own thoughts and feelings due to what they saw. Secretary Chang, who was accompanying them, didn't say much. While everyone was silent, the car passed through a village. In this village, there were also several families with only four walls. (15)

Tidbits 13

— (Echo)

It is common for women to apply powder and perfume to their faces and hair, and it is not surprising: this is a phenomenon that should exist for those who want to please. But the fact that the perfume from unknown sources is applied to the powder legs makes me feel that the world is indeed "getting worse every day," and the sense of smell of the men in the world is also becoming more and more degenerate!

Successful People in the City 14

— Holding Buddha

Everyone knows that diligence and thrift are the "road to success"; however, there are many roads to success in the city, not just the two roads of "diligence" and "thrift." Perhaps only knowing to take these two roads may not lead to success; there may be times of hitting a wall.

Thirty years ago, there were three street urchins, A, B, and C, who lived a wandering life in S City, scavenging, picking up cigarette butts, and pulling oxen across the bridge, which were their only occupations. One day, they had no money to buy snacks to fill their stomachs, and their stomachs were growling like thunder. Urchin A calmly ran to a rice cake stall, wanting to borrow 120 coins for three rice cakes so that the three of them could share them. The owner of the rice cake stall glanced at him and saw that he was a street urchin, so he wouldn't lend him anything. Urchin A ran back dejectedly, discussing how to deal with the situation. Urchins B and C ran to the rice cake stall and started a fight on purpose. Urchin A took the opportunity to grab a handful of copper coins and ran away. Urchins B and C also scattered. This time, the problem of running out of food was finally solved.

One winter, these three urchins suddenly had good luck. In the snow, they saw an old man, reeking of alcohol, staggering into an alley. They saw that the old man was drunk and not very clear-headed; without hesitation, they swarmed up and carried out their specialty, the "pig-skinning" job. It was also their fate to have good luck. In addition to stripping off the squirrel fur coat and fox fur robe, they also grabbed more than 300 yuan in banknotes from the pocket. The three urchins were dazzled and couldn't close their eyes from laughing. The old man was still confused and thought someone was playing tug-of-war with him. After struggling for a while, he fell to the ground like a dead pig.

The three urchins, A, B, and C, had smooth sailing from then on. Each of them used the money they had plundered as a fund. In addition to doing some legitimate business, they still did some special business from time to time. Now, these three brothers all have family property, concubines, and cars. Their daily income is really not small.

"Everyone can do magic, but each has their own tricks." Isn't the success of the A, B, and C urchins taking a different path? Now, young people are shouting about "unemployment," "hunger," and "recession." It's really a sign of weakness if they don't know how to "strike while the iron is cold."

Ullambana Festival 15

— Yan Biguang

This summer, the countryside, shrouded in superstition, has been lifting out the Dragon King to pray for rain and exposing the copper Guanyin to the hot sun. Drumming and gongs, they held god-welcoming events every day, and until now, they have forgotten even the season of falling autumn. The cracks in the rice fields are five or six inches wide, and the food waiting to be replanted, such as buckwheat and mung beans, cannot be planted. It is really frantic.

The general farmers, seeing that there is no hope for the autumn harvest, rumors are spreading like wildfire, such as zombies causing trouble, passing Yin soldiers, saying many superstitious words, not worth a smile from those who know!

Not having rice at home to cook is not a big deal, but the Ullambana Festival is a top priority. Every family sells their clothes to collect money, hire some monks to chant scriptures and recite Buddhist prayers, the sound is clear and melodious, the Sanskrit sounds match, and they also paste a lot of paper clothes, paper trousers, and paper utensils to burn, squandering useful money in the void. They believe that the Buddhist Dharma is boundless and can relieve all the suffering of the victims, relying on heaven to eat. But they are willing to chew on grass roots and bark, which is really ridiculously foolish.

The lunar seventh month is said to be a ghost season. In the past, there were also Buddhist events and burnings. But this year, even people have no money to spend and no rice to eat, but people are still very enthusiastic, holding Ullambana festivals every day - performing public offerings - isn't it a strange thing? Even the burning of paper money and tin foil is an even more considerable loss of money!

— Yin Juan

Random Talk

Modern Curiosities 17

— Yao Zhongyin

The two characters "摩登" (módēng), or "modern," have been used in China for quite some time and are commonly understood as "fashionable"! Regarding "fashionable" as "modern," the more "modern" one becomes, the more harmful it is! However, according to the original French, "modern" is translated as "contemporary." If we take "contemporary" to be "modern," the more "modern" one becomes, the more beneficial it is! I cannot help but feel moved by this. I have often said that everything is good when it's in a foreign country, but it turns bad once it arrives in China! This is not just the case with the characters "摩登." Although Director Wang tries hard to correct it, the ingrained habit is too deep, and people continue to be unaware. It's difficult to see results without a thorough and fundamental reform. I will try to explore its origin, curb its flow, reveal its confusion, and point out its mistakes. When things reach an extreme, they will inevitably reverse, so perhaps there is still hope!

Examining the "Records of Mochou Lake," Volume Six, "Verifications of the Words of the Yujin Hall," the "Wanghai Tide" poem by Che Qiuling contains two lines: "Remaining fashionable and wondrous appearance, Zhou Fang could depict." The two characters "摩登" appear in the writings of a poet. When "摩登" is described as "wondrous appearance," it clearly refers to a woman. This poem was originally written about a young married woman of the Lu family by Mochou Lake. According to the "Records of Famous Paintings Through the Ages" and the "Xuanhe Painting Catalogue," "Zhou Fang, styled Jingxuan, was skilled at painting women, often in a plump and dignified manner." As the "Verifications of the Words of the Yujin Hall" was compiled by Ma Jucun during the Qing Jiaqing period, it is known that the term "摩登" has been used for a long time.

Also, examining the "Surangama Sutra": "Shakyamuni's cousin, Ananda, encountered the Matangi woman, was led into her chamber of debauchery, and was about to break his vows!" The name of Matangi was Prakriti, a prostitute! Even though Ananda was already a disciple of the Buddha, how could a disciple of the Buddha encounter a prostitute? Could it be that a prostitute is also an incarnation of the Buddha? Ananda means "joy." When the Joyful Buddha meets Matangi, could the Joyful Buddha in the Yonghe Temple be a transformation of this Buddha? Matangi was a prostitute, so why would people embrace this and insist on pursuing "摩登"? The Buddha's original intention was to universally save all beings. Is this also meant to serve as a warning? Buddhist texts also say that "men are called Matanga, and women are called Matangizhi. Prakriti is the Matangi woman. The Matangi woman and modern women are one and two, two and one." There is a reason for imitation.

"摩登" in China is like this, while "modern" in foreign countries is like that. China's pursuit of "摩登" leads to gradual degeneration, while foreign countries' pursuit of "modern" leads to gradual evolution. Different perspectives result in different behaviors, and the facts become vastly different. China lags behind foreign countries in everything. Even when it comes to "摩登," it is far behind foreign countries. Not only is it far behind, but it also goes against the grain. Perpetuating errors leads to further errors, and where will this lead us? To correct this error, we should use the term "contemporary" to rescue "fashionable." It is better to be a "contemporary woman" than a "fashionable woman." What contemporary women need are: education, profession, consistent career, and indispensability. Strive for a new lifestyle in clothing, food, housing, and transportation; promote domestic goods; advocate simplicity, love cleanliness, uphold thrift, and admire competence. Only then can we be worthy of being called a "contemporary woman"! Only then can we be worthy of being called a truly "modern" woman! Those who study "摩登" today must distinguish clearly between the old and the new!

Mourning Zhu Rongjing at Sea 18

— Yuan Chu

Life values affinity; those of different kinds cannot mingle. I knew you in the early days of Renzi, when your literary talent chased after pure joy. Although our unrestrained temperaments differed, we understood each other perfectly. In the midst of wine, our words were sincere, often engraved in our hearts. Shiqiao was filled with the setting sun, the name of the street where you lived.

The autumn wind at the edge of the sea is cold. I came to sit and have a deep conversation, hastily arranging cups and dishes. Our farewell was always hurried, the meaning never fully explained. Twenty years pass in the blink of an eye, and now you are in a coffin. I recognized the tracks at the door, still bearing the marks of the year before. Ascending to the hall and relying on the spirit altar, the sight fills me with sorrow. I awkwardly offer condolences to the young children, silently watching. Returning feels like a lifetime ago; who can dry these tears?

Records of Imperial Fragrance, Vaguely Floating 19

— Original work by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

The two effects it had were: (1) to isolate it from the Tianjin train station, and (2) to prevent the Empress Dowager's jade feet from touching the soil trod upon by ordinary people. Needless to say, the person who came up with this plan must have been a very clever character! Dear readers, can you guess who this clever character was? Mentioning this person's great name, I don't think anyone wouldn't know him, right? This person was none other than Mr. Yuan Shikai of Xiangcheng, who will forever occupy a very important page in Chinese history! At that time, he was serving as the Governor-General of Zhili Province. Before the Empress Dowager set off south from Beijing, he had already decided to hold a grand welcoming ceremony and build a new platform.

The length of this platform was very long, although it could not accommodate the entire imperial train, it was enough for ten cars. On top of it, there was a bamboo shed covered with reed mats, and the shed was covered with countless dragon flags and other flags, as well as colorful ribbons, green pine and cypress trees, and various palace lanterns, which were decorated very beautifully and movingly. The ground was naturally covered with golden yellow sand. And on a square of land in the center, another apricot-yellow carpet was laid, which was prepared for the Empress Dowager to stand on after getting off the train. However, even though they were designing it like this, no one dared to determine whether the Empress Dowager would really be willing to get off the train when she arrived in Tianjin. Even a minister as powerful as Yuan Shikai did not dare to say, "The Empress Dowager must get off the train here."

The platform was newly built, the ground had yellow sand, and the top had a brightly lit reed shed. Naturally, it was very magnificent! From afar, we leaned out of the car window to look at it, and everyone found it very pleasing to the eye and couldn't help but compete to watch. And our train was gradually preparing to stop. (124)
