The Bond Market Trended Upwards Last Week

Gains Ranged from Over 1 Yuan to 3.23 Yuan

Last week, from September 3rd to 8th, the Shanghai Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange gradually started to trend upwards after the situation turned slightly better the previous week. This was because the foreign exchange interbank rate gradually decreased, decreasing by 6 points in a week. The outflow of cash stopped because international silver prices gradually became balanced. The situation between Japan and Russia suddenly eased after being extremely tense. The Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Committee was held as scheduled, and there were no problems. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek had already recovered his health, and the rumors were completely quelled. It was also heard that a certain bank would release 20% of its 40% cash reserve for banknotes to circulate in the market, and the shortfall would be made up with government bonds. The Bank Savings Law was about to be implemented. The foreign exchange interbank rate was expected to fall, and short sellers panicked. Table and northern speculators were the earliest and most aggressive in covering their short positions, and the market price rebounded. Intermediate table speculators turned short, but found that they could not apply their skills to suppress the market. The trend should continue to rise, and the saying that the 96 bonds would be reorganized had a cause but no factual basis, as it was not yet the time. Over the past week, the foreign exchange interbank rate rose by 1 point on Monday, but the environment improved, the atmosphere between Japan and Russia eased, and silver was gradually no longer a problem. Northern speculators first covered their short positions, and the market price suddenly turned around, recovering several jiao to over 1 yuan. The foreign exchange interbank rate continued to fall on Tuesday, and the upward trend was strong. There were full-day gains, with the 6th reorganization bond being the strongest, rising by 2.75 yuan. The upward trend continued on Wednesday, but the closing price fell by over 1 yuan due to a temporary disruption of telecommunications between Fujian and Shanghai, but the result was still a gain of several jiao to over 1 yuan. Almost half of the previous losses were recovered, which again caused table speculators to sell short, and the 4th also saw selling. The price rebounded by a small amount of jiao to 1 yuan on Thursday. On Friday, the report on the central government's financial situation was good. The 96 government bonds suddenly rose by 1 yuan, and the others also turned upwards by several jiao to over 1 yuan. The initial gains were still strong on Saturday, but then rebounded slightly. As a result, the gains and losses were uneven. As a result of the week's market prices, gains ranged from several jiao to 3.23 yuan. The total number of transactions was 154,833,000 yuan. New York Dollar Stocks Are Particularly Good

The Sun Fung Company reported that yesterday (8th) the New York stock market was sluggish due to low trading volume, so various stocks fell in a mixed manner. Generally, commercial news was better than before. Small exchange stocks were mixed, bonds fell and were mixed, but the dollar was quite strong. Half-day trading volume was 210,000 shares. Yarn and Cotton

American Cotton Was Mixed and Unstable

The market for American and Japanese cotton was mixed and unstable while awaiting government reports. It was initially firm due to good news from Liverpool, but then weakened due to long positions being closed. As a result, spot prices rose by 5 points, while futures prices fluctuated between gains and losses of 1 to 5 points. English cotton futures rose by 3 to 5 points. Indian cotton rose due to buying and short covering by brokers. As a result, Pingguoer rose by 7.5 jiao, and Aomula and Bailuoxi rose by 1.5 rupee. Second U.S. Government Cotton Crop Report

—An Increase of 57,000 Bales Compared to the First—

Washington, 8th - The second cotton crop estimate was officially released by the Bureau of Agricultural Economics at noon today. The production percentage is 53.8, and the output is 9,252,000 bales, an increase of 57,000 bales compared to the previous estimate. The conditions for the same period in the previous six years are also recorded on the left (unit: thousand bales):

Grains

Sutong Japonica Plummeted by 2-3 Jiao

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the supply from various sources suddenly increased, with over 20 dealers arriving (a total of 3,450 shi of goods), mostly thick japonica rice. Late rice was indeed in the minority, and sales were still sluggish. Therefore, with this surge in supply, people panicked, and the market situation deteriorated. For example, Sutong japonica rice plummeted by 2 jiao. Fortunately, common varieties such as Nangang rice and late rice were scarce and still soft. In addition, new japonica and new pointed rice continued to fall by over 1-2 jiao. Yinbianyuan also fell by a small amount of 2-3 jiao, and fragrant rice was not spared.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were 23-24 dealers from various sources down the river. There was some trading of shorter-priced goods on the market. The market price for white japonica was high, and the medium and low prices were down by a small amount of 1 jiao. Early thin rice was high, and the medium and low prices were down by a small amount of 2 jiao. Dongxin japonica was down by a small amount of 2 jiao. Chen Yang Dujian was tired and cheap. The arrival of new Yang Dujian continued to be strong, but the price was not good, and the price was down by a small amount of 2-3 jiao. Bairyuan new and old guest points were also tired by several fen. Twenty shi of Xixin japonica arrived today. The rice quality was inferior to last year, and the price opened at 11.8 yuan.
